***вносить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a> (6364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnosítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внести.html>внести́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to carry in, to bring in</li>
<li>to pay in, to deposit</li>
<li>to bring in / about, to cause, to introduce
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разлад.html>разла́д</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:семья.html>семью́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> razlád v semʹjú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cause dissension in the family</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ошибка.html>оши́бку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> ošíbku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to introduce an error</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:оживление.html>оживле́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> oživlénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to brighten up</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспорядок.html>беспоря́док</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> besporjádok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to cause disorder, to bring about disorder</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to enter, to include, to insert
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:усовершенствование.html>усоверше́нствование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> usoveršénstvovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to introduce an improvement</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изменение.html>измене́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> izmenénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make alterations / changes</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поправка.html>попра́вки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> poprávki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to insert / introduce amendments (into)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:список.html>спи́сок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> v spísok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to enter in the list, to put on the list, enroll</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to move, to bring in, to bring / put forward, to submit, to table
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вносить.html>вноси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:законопроект.html>законопрое́кт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnosítʹ</b> zakonoproékt</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to introduce a bill</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(in expressions)

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:вноситься.html>вноси́ться</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4c.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — внести́сь.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́тренний</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vnútrennij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренность.html>вну́тренность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnútrennostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренность.html>вну́тренности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренность.html>вну́тренности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внутренность.html>вну́тренностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>interior, inside</li>
<li><i>pl.</i> internal organs, innards, viscera, entrails, intestines, bowels, garbage, interior</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<p><b>вну́т<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>рен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ность</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

***внучка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:внучек.html>внучка</a> (16822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внук.html>внук</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vnuk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">вънукъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭnukŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъnukъ</i>
</p>

***внушать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a> (5268)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vnušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnušátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arouse (fear, etc.), to instill/inspire (respect, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́х</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> komú-libo stráx</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to arouse fear in someone</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:уважение.html>уваже́ние</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> komú-libo uvažénije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to command someone's respect</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to convince, to suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́л</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ...</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nam <b>vnušíl</b>, što ...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He convinced us that ...</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> кому́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> myslʹ komú-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to suggest an idea to someone</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>вну<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ша́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
<a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>Внуша́ть</a> + <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дата.html>да́т</a>. п.</i>; <a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a> + <i><a href = vnd.unilang:вино.html>ви́н</a>. п.</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:внушивший.html>внуши́вший</a> (7884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушивший.html>внуши́вший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnušívšij</span>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́ть</a> (7884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">въноушити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vŭnušiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnušítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to arouse (fear, etc.), to instill/inspire (respect, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>стра́х</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> komú-libo stráx</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to arouse fear in someone</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> кому́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:уважение.html>уваже́ние</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> komú-libo uvažénije</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to command someone's respect</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to convince, to suggest
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нам</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушить.html>внуши́л</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> ...</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On nam <b>vnušíl</b>, što ...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He convinced us that ...</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внушать.html>внуша́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мысль</a> кому́-либо</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnušátʹ</b> myslʹ komú-libo</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to suggest an idea to someone</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***внять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:внять.html>внять</a> (17011)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъnęti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъ(n)-</i> (see <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*vъ(n)</i>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ęti</i>. Reanalyzed as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:невдомек.html>в-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from which other words in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-нять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-njatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> were created, such as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нанять.html>наня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nanjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:обнять.html>обня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">obnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внять.html>внять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vnjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:внимать.html>внима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> poetic or stilted</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to listen (to); to hear; to hark (to); to hearken; to heed, to pay heed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:внять.html>вня́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́тве</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vnjátʹ</b> molítve</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to hear the/a prayer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почему.html>почему́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:внять.html>вня́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>мои́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совет.html>сове́там</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Počemú ty ne <b>vnjal</b> moím sovétam?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Why didn't you pay heed to my advice?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> (82)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_2">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">location</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> in, at, on <i>(+ prepositional case)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">direction</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to, into <i>(+ accusative case)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">time</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> at, in, on</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>The form <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></span> is used before some awkward consonant clusters, such as <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:второй.html>второ́м</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вторник.html>вто́рник</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> флори́де</span>. In most cases, use <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> instead.</li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Particle">Particle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clipped form of <a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вобрать.html>вобра́ть</a> (15816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">во-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:брать.html>брать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bratʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вобрать.html>вобра́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vobrátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вбирать.html>вбира́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to absorb, to imbibe</li>
<li>to suck in, to drink in</li>
<li>to inhale</li></ol>

***вовлекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вовлекать.html>вовлека́ть</a> (25844)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вовлек-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vovlek-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вовлекать.html>вовлека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vovlekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вовлечь.html>вовле́чь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to involve (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, in)</li>
<li>to drag into, to embroil</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>вле<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ка́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:вовлечь.html>вовле́чь</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>во-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-влек-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
